# 15) Who owns what

* **Docs PM**: roadmap, IA, KPIs.
* **Tech Writers** (embedded with squads): author/review feature docs.
* **SMEs**: provide truth & examples; approve accuracy.
* **DevRel**: SDK/Marketplace, samples, tutorials.
* **Compliance**: templates, evidence pack docs, audits.
* **SRE**: runbooks, SLO references, incident templates.
* **Security**: threat models, policy docs, hardening guides.



Awesome—here’s a concrete, “ready-to-build” expansion of the **Platform Services (Shared)**. For each capability you’ll get: purpose, architecture, data/contracts, key APIs/CLIs, events, SLOs/NFRs, security/operational guardrails, KPIs, and acceptance tests.

---

# Identity & Access

**Purpose**
Single sign-on, lifecycle provisioning (SCIM), and fine-grained authorization (ABAC) with explainable policy outcomes.

**Architecture**

* **AuthN**: OIDC/OAuth2 (enterprise IdP; fallback Keycloak).
* **Directory**: internal tenant directory (users, groups, roles, service accounts).
* **AuthZ**: OPA sidecar (Rego) + decision cache; attributes from resource + user claims.
* **Policy Simulator**: “why denied?” service (replays inputs; explains Rego decision path).

**Core data**
`User{ id, sub, email, groups[], roles[] }`
`Policy{ id, package, rego, version, scope }`
`ResourceAttrs{ type, tenant, project, classification, exportControl, owner, variant }`

**APIs**

* `POST /auth/introspect` (token → claims)
* `POST /authz/evaluate` (subject, action, resourceAttrs) → ALLOW/DENY + reasons
* `POST /scim/v2/Users|Groups` (provisioning)
* `GET /policies/{id}/simulate?user=...&action=...&resource=...`

**Events**
`UserProvisioned`, `GroupChanged`, `PolicyUpdated`, `AccessDenied` (audited)

**SLOs/NFRs**

* AuthZ decision P95 ≤ **10 ms** (cached).
* Propagation (SCIM→can log in) ≤ **5 min**.

**Security/ops**

* JTI replay protection; PKCE for public clients; token lifetime short + refresh.
* OPA bundles signed; policy PRs require review + tests.

**KPIs**
Policy denials explained ratio (= 100%); mean “time-to-unblock” after denial < 15 min.

**Acceptance**
Adding a user to “Approvers” in IdP enables approvals in ≤ 5 min; simulator shows exact missing attribute when denied.

---

# Workflow

**Purpose**
Durable, observable business processes (ECR/ECO, CAPA, approvals) and technical sagas.

**Architecture**

* **Temporal** for micro-workflows & retries.
* **BPMN** engine (Camunda/Zeebe) for business flows (visual models).
* **Audit stream** of all state transitions.

**APIs**

* `POST /workflows/{type}/start {input}` → `{runId}`
* `POST /workflows/{runId}/signal {name,payload}`
* `GET /workflows/{runId}/history`
* `POST /bpmn/instances` (start from BPMN key + variables)

**Events**
`WorkflowStarted|Completed|Failed`, `TaskWaiting`, `ApprovalRequested|Granted|Rejected`

**SLOs**
Task dispatch P95 ≤ **200 ms**; cron triggers ± **2 s** jitter.

**Security/ops**

* Idempotent start (business key).
* Compensating steps for external writes; heartbeat timeouts with escalation.

**KPIs**
% workflows finishing without manual intervention; average approval wait.

**Acceptance**
If an approval activity times out, escalation path triggers a second approver and leaves an audit entry.

---

# Rules & DMN

**Purpose**
Configurable decisions (approver routing, variant resolution, risk scoring) decoupled from code.

**Architecture**

* DMN engine (Kogito/Camunda DMN) + in-memory cache, versioned tables.
* Rule bundles signed and promoted via GitOps.

**APIs**

* `POST /rules/{table}/evaluate {inputs}` → `{decision, rationale}`
* `POST /rules/bundles` (upload) | `GET /rules/bundles/{ver}`

**Events**
`RuleBundlePublished`, `DecisionEvaluated` (sampled for tracing)

**SLOs**
Decision evaluation P95 ≤ **5 ms** (hot cache).

**Security/ops**

* Rule inputs/outputs classified; PII minimization; regression tests required per change.

**KPIs**
Hit-rate per branch; override rate (human overrides) < 5%.

**Acceptance**
Changing routing rule instantly affects next review request, and simulator shows which row matched.

---

# Event Backbone

**Purpose**
Reliable, auditable eventing fabric with schemas, compatibility, DLQs, and replay.

**Architecture**

* Kafka (multi-AZ) + **Schema Registry** (Avro/Protobuf).
* **Outbox** pattern per service (Tx publish).
* **DLQ** per topic; **Replay** tool (bounded by time/offset).

**Topic taxonomy**
`dom.{context}.{aggregate}.evt` — canonical domain events
`int.{system}.cdc` — raw connector feeds
`ops.audit` — audit events

**Contracts**

* SemVer; **backward-compatible** MINOR/PATCH enforced by CI.
* Envelopes: `eventId, eventType, aggregateId, tenantId, occurredAt, actor, schemaVersion, hash, classifications`.

**Ops**

* Idempotent consumers with dedupe store; partition key = aggregateId.
* Quotas + per-tenant rate limits.

**SLOs**
Producer→consumer median < **500 ms**; P95 < **2 s** (in-region).

**KPIs**
DLQ depth, schema compat violations, consumer lag.

**Acceptance**
Replaying 1 day of `ChangeApproved` reproduces identical baselines; no duplicate side effects.

---

# Search & Discovery

**Purpose**
Fast, secure search for artifacts with domain-aware ranking.

**Architecture**

* OpenSearch clusters; **index-per-view** projections.
* **Security filtering**: document contains ACL/attributes; filtered at query time.
* Synonyms & analyzers per domain; autocomplete service.

**APIs**

* `GET /search?q=...&type=Requirement&filters=...`
* `POST /indices/{view}/reindex`
* `GET /suggest?q=bra` → `["brake", "bracket"]`

**Events**
`ProjectionUpdated`, `IndexStale` (monitors)

**SLOs**
Query P95 ≤ **2 s**; autocomplete < **100 ms**.

**KPIs**
Click-through, zero-result rate, median freshness (event→indexed) < **60 s**.

**Acceptance**
Changing a requirement title makes it discoverable via new string in ≤ 60 s; secure results hide export-controlled items.

---

# File/Model Store

**Purpose**
Durable object storage with dedupe, scanning, watermarking, and secure viewers (PDF/CAD).

**Architecture**

* S3-compatible object store (versioned, per-tenant buckets/keys).
* **Content-addressed** (SHA-256) objects; dedupe index.
* Antivirus/DLP scanners; media service for thumbnails and viewer prep.
* CAD/PDF viewers (JT/glTF; PDF renderer) with **no raw download** option.

**APIs**

* `POST /files` (multipart or signed URL init) → `{objectId, sha256, size}`
* `GET /files/{id}` (stream; policy-checked)
* `POST /shares` (watermarked, expiring external link)
* `POST /renders/cad` → lightweight render

**Events**
`FileStored`, `ScanFailed`, `ShareCreated|Expired`.

**SLOs**
Upload init < **100 ms**; render preview ready < **2 s** for medium assets.

**Security/ops**

* Server-side encryption (per-tenant KMS); watermark overlays; viewer session tokens; range reads; WORM (for evidence).

**KPIs**
Dedup ratio, scan failure rate, external share usage (with expiry).

**Acceptance**
Uploading a CAD file stores single deduped object across duplicates; supplier link is watermarked and expires on time.

---

# Graph/Thread

**Purpose**
Authoritative cross-domain traceability graph powering impact, evidence, and lineage.

**Architecture**

* Graph DB (Neo4j/JanusGraph).
* **Ingest only from events** (CQRS); no direct writes from UIs.
* **Signed baselines**: Merkle tree over node/edge set + DSSE signatures.

**Model**
Nodes: `Requirement, DesignItem, Part, TestCase, TestRun, Change, WI, Twin, Document, Baseline...`
Edges: `derivesFrom, satisfies, implements, verifies, allocatedTo, mitigates, affectsVariant, asBuiltOf, asMaintainedOf ...` (+ attributes: createdBy, confidence, justification)

**APIs**

* `GET /graph/impact?id=REQ-123&hops=5`
* `POST /baselines` (snapshot + sign)
* `GET /baselines/{id}/diff?vs=...`

**Events**
`BaselineCreated`, `TraceLinkAdded|Removed`, `ImpactComputed` (async cache warmers)

**SLOs**
Impact traversal (≤10k neighborhood) P95 ≤ **30 s**; point lookups ≤ **200 ms**.

**Security/ops**

* ABAC filter at query layer; link creation only via domain services; SHACL constraints.
* Baseline rehydrate tooling; tamper-evident hash logs.

**KPIs**
Trace coverage %, baseline verify pass rate, average impact size.

**Acceptance**
Given a changed requirement, the graph service returns affected tests/parts/WIs in under 30 s and the signed baseline verifies.

---

# NLG/NLP

**Purpose**
Generate/assist documentation: evidence packs, release notes, summaries, gap detection, entity extraction.

**Architecture**

* Templating engine (Handlebars/Jinja) + **graph queries**.
* NLG workers (stateless) with policy-controlled prompts; **no PII** in prompts; content filters.
* NLP utilities: schema-guided extraction, similarity, gap detection.

**APIs**

* `POST /nlg/generate {templateId, baselineId, scope, params}` → `{docId}`
* `POST /nlp/extract {model, text}`
* `POST /nlp/gap-detect {artifactIds[]}`

**Events**
`DocumentGenerated`, `GapDetected`.

**SLOs**
Evidence pack P95 ≤ **2 min**; short summaries < **3 s**.

**Security/ops**

* Deterministic templates prioritized; AI outputs flagged “assisted”; human review required for external docs; watermarking.
* Prompt library versioned; redaction layer pre-prompt.

**KPIs**
Manual edit ratio < 10% for standard packs; gap true-positive rate.

**Acceptance**
Generating a V&V pack at baseline B produces identical outputs when re-run; verifier confirms signatures.

# Observability

**Purpose**
End-to-end telemetry: traces, metrics, logs, topology, SLO/error-budget management.

**Architecture**

* OTel collectors (daemonset + gateway).
* Metrics: Prometheus; Logs: Loki; Traces: Tempo/Jaeger; Dashboards: Grafana.
* **SLO manager**: recording rules + burn alerts + runbook links.
* **Topology** from service spans + mesh.

**APIs/CLIs**

* `POST /slo` (create SLO spec), `GET /topology`, `GET /alerts`.
* Grafana/Alertmanager as-code repos.

**SLIs/SLOs**

* Read P95 targets, availability, consumer lag, outbox drain, etc. (per service).

**Security/ops**

* PII/secret scrubbing; auth on dashboards; multi-tenant labels (tenantId).
* Tail-sampling to control cost.

**KPIs**
SLO compliance %, mean time to detect/resolve, alert fatigue (pages/month), cost per GB.

**Acceptance**
A burst of 5xx raises a fast-burn alert with a runbook link; canary automatically rolls back via auto-remediation workflow.

---

# Secrets & KMS

**Purpose**
Centralized, auditable secret and key management.

**Architecture**

* Vault + KMS (per-tenant keys); secrets via CSI; dynamic DB creds; envelope encryption lib.

**APIs**

* `POST /secrets` (create/update metadata), `GET /secrets/{path}` (brokered to Vault),
* `POST /kms/encrypt|decrypt` (for services without SDK).

**Policies**

* Least privilege; time-boxed tokens; secret rotation schedules; sealed-secrets for GitOps.

**SLOs**
Secret fetch P95 ≤ **30 ms** (cache); rotation completion windows (< 48 h) tracked.

**KPIs**
Rotation compliance 100%; zero plaintext secrets in repos.

**Acceptance**
Rotating DB creds causes zero downtime (DB pool rollover); audit shows no use of expired creds.

# Policy & Compliance

**Purpose**
Guardrails for clusters, data handling, residency, retention, and release compliance.

**Architecture**

* **OPA/Gatekeeper** for cluster policies (image signatures, non-root, network policies).
* **Data policies**: residency & retention enforcers (OPA + scheduled jobs).
* **Release policy**: gates for SBOM, signatures, evidence.

**Policies (examples)**

* “Only signed images (cosign) may run.”
* “Export-controlled items cannot be shared externally.”
* “Evidence bundles: WORM + 10-year retention.”
* “EU tenant data must stay in EU region.”

**APIs**

* `POST /policy/validate {kind, specimen}` → decision + rationale
* `GET /policy/violations` (feed dashboards)
* `POST /retention/run?dataset=...` (on-demand)

**Events**
`PolicyViolation`, `RetentionJobCompleted`, `ResidencyBreachBlocked`.

**SLOs**
Admission decision ≤ **10 ms**; policy update rollout ≤ **15 min**.

**KPIs**
Zero Sev-1 policy escapes; violation mean time to remediate; % workloads signed.

**Acceptance**
Deploying an unsigned image is rejected with actionable reason; moving EU tenant data to non-EU bucket is blocked and logged.

# Shell & Navigation

**Goals**

* Give every discipline the same mental model (Discover → Define → Design → Verify → Deliver → Operate).
* Keep power users fast (command palette/shortcuts) and new users oriented (guided nav, help).

**Architecture**

* **Shell app** (React, Module Federation host) composes MFEs at runtime.
* **BFF** (GraphQL gateway for reads + REST for mutations) shapes “screen models.”
* **Route contracts**: `/discover`, `/define`, `/design`, `/verify`, `/deliver`, `/operate`.

**Global UI**

* **Top bar**: lifecycle tabs, global search, command palette (⌘/Ctrl-K), notifications, help, profile, tenant/env badges.
* **Left rail**: context nav (projects/products/programs), saved views, recents.
* **Right drawer**: **Trace panel**, **Activity/Comments**, **Properties**.

**Global Search**

* Federated index (OpenSearch) with **type-ahead** by `id/title/tag`, filters (type/state/owner/project/baseline).
* Quick actions from results (open, copy link, start review, start change).

**Command Palette**

* Universal verbs: “Create Requirement,” “Start Change,” “Generate Evidence Pack,” “Open by ID,” “Run Impact Analysis.”
* Extensible registry (MFEs contribute commands with `canExecute` predicates).

**Notifications/Inbox**

* Real-time (SSE/websocket) + digests.
* Types: mentions, reviews, approvals, status changes, KPI breaches. Snooze/mute per thread.

**Help**

* Contextual docs (route + role), glossary hovercards, mini-tours, feedback widget.

**Non-functionals**

* P95 route change ≤ 1.0s; LCP ≤ 2.5s; a11y WCAG 2.1 AA; i18n (ICU), RTL-ready.

# Micro-Frontends (MFEs)

**Catalog**

* Requirements, Change, Test/V&V, BOM/Parts, Simulation, Quality, Compliance, Portfolio, Ops, Twins, Docs.

**Contract**

* Each MFE exports: `mount()`, `manifest.json` (routes, capabilities, permissions, feature flags, i18n packs).
* **Data access**: GraphQL (federated schema) for reads; REST/gRPC for commands; events via SSE/websocket.
* **State**: server-state first (React Query), optimistic writes only for safe ops (comments, tags).

**Common components (shared lib)**

* Data grid (virtualized), tree, diff viewer (fields/files/graph), approvals rail, checklist, doc viewer, CAD/3D viewer, trace panel, comment thread.

**Security & Policy**

* OIDC in shell; **ABAC hints** fetched per view to hide/disable controls; “Why can’t I?” explainer via policy simulator.

**Quality**

* A11y tests (axe-core), visual regression (Storybook/Chromatic), bundle budget per route (< 250 KB gz where possible).

# Review & Approvals

**Use cases**

* Artifact review (req/spec/test/part/BOM), change approval (ECR/ECO), supplier package acceptance, doc sign-off.

**Data model**

* `Review { id, artifactRefs[], type, state, checklistTemplateId, checklistItems[], approvers[], requiredQuorum, dueAt, signatures[], auditTrail[] }`
* `Signature { userId, method (eIDAS/ESIGN), time, certificateRef, reason }`

**Workflow**

1. Start review → select artifacts/scope → attach **checklist** template.
2. System pre-fills **evidence** (coverage %, open issues, risk flags).
3. Route to approvers (DMN rules by classification/criticality).
4. Approvers see **diff view** (fields, relations, files) + must leave rationale.
5. Upon quorum, system:

   * Stamps **baseline** (cryptographic hash + DSSE).
   * Emits `ReviewApproved`, `BaselineCreated`.
   * Locks relevant versions and updates V&V matrix / evidence packs.

**E-signatures**

* Standards: ESIGN/eIDAS. Capture certificate, IP, timestamp, hash of content. Verifiable via downloadable manifest.

**Checklists**

* Template per artifact type/standard (Safety, Compliance, QA). Items can be auto-satisfied by live metrics (e.g., “Coverage ≥ 90%”).
* Exceptions require justification and escalate automatically.

**KPIs**

* MTTApprove (mean time to approve), approval SLA adherence, % reviews using checklists, % approvals with complete evidence.

**Acceptance tests**

* Starting a review auto-fills evidence; signing produces a verifiable package (manifest hash matches); baseline rebuild reproduces content byte-for-byte.

---

# Comments & Decision Logs

**Inline Comments**

* Anchors: text ranges, form fields, table cells, code diffs, CAD viewport regions (bbox/face IDs), images.
* Rich content: @mentions, #artifact links, code fences, attachments (hash-stored), emoji.
* Visibility: public/project/private; external-share with watermark & expiry.

**Decision Logs (ADRs)**

* Lightweight ADRs linked to artifacts: `ADR { id, context, options, decision, consequences, owners, status, reviewAt }`
* Surfacing: local “Decisions” tab + global timeline; search by topic/component.

**Moderation & Etiquette**

* Resolve threads; archive stale; mention policies; escalation ladder for blocking items.

**Events**

* `CommentAdded`, `CommentResolved`, `DecisionLogged`, `DecisionSuperseded`.

**KPIs**

* Comment response SLA, unresolved threads aging, % changes with decision logs.

**Acceptance tests**

* Create comment on CAD face → saved anchor reflows after CAD update but remains on same face ID; mentioned user receives notification and can reply inline.

---

# Document Workspace

**Editors**

* **Spec Editor**: schema-driven sections, tables, references to artifacts (live chips), variables (`{{baseline.id}}`), change tracking.
* **Drawing Viewer**: PDF/CAD lightweight renders (JT/glTF); pan/zoom, layers, measurements, region comments, redaction overlays.
* **Report Composer**: templates (Markdown/Handlebars) + graph queries → assemble V&V matrices, change summaries, safety cases, release notes.
* **Release Notes**: diff between baselines; NLG summarization; edit passes; export.

**Bindings & NLG**

* Live bindings pull data at render time from the Thread graph (with baseline pinning).
* NLG modules generate narrative sections (e.g., “impact summary”) under author control.

**Export & Distribution**

* PDF/HTML with watermarking, page seals (hash), embedded manifest link; external share links with expiry.
* **Signing**: DSSE sign manifest + PDF hash; verifier CLI.

**Versioning**

* Docs have revisions tied to **baselines**; diff viewer shows data and prose changes.

**KPIs**

* Generation P95 ≤ 2 min; % documents with live bindings; manual edit ratio for standard packs.

**Acceptance tests**

* Generate evidence pack for baseline B42 → hash stable across re-renders; opening in verifier confirms signature and provenance.

# Supplier Portal

**Purpose**

* Enable external partners to collaborate safely: upload design packages, participate in reviews, receive scoped work.

**Access & Scope**

* **Just-enough visibility**: project/lineage-scoped lists; attribute redaction (e.g., cost, proprietary features).
* **Identity**: external IdP/OIDC; per-supplier roles; audit-heavy.

**Package Intake**

* Upload bundle (CAD/STEP/PDF/spec/test results); system runs:

  * **Interface checks** (geometry/tolerances, metadata completeness).
  * **Policy checks** (classification/export control).
  * Virus scan & DLP.

**Automated Interface Checks**

* Rules engine compares supplier CAD against interface contracts (hole patterns, mating surfaces, envelope).
* Emits `SupplierCheckFailed` items with annotated viewer callouts.

**Redacted Viewers**

* View-only streams (no raw CAD download); watermarking, screenshot deterrence, region comment support.

**Collaboration**

* Structured reviews with checklists; comment threads; delegated approvals (internal sponsor signs final).

**Deliverable Acceptance**

* On acceptance, system creates/updates Part/BOM, links evidence, and stamps supplier delivery baseline.

**KPIs**

* Supplier onboarding time (< 48h), package turnaround time, interface check pass rate, policy violation rate (target zero).

**Acceptance tests**

* Supplier uploads CAD → interface check identifies two violations with on-model callouts → supplier fixes → automated recheck passes → internal approver signs → MBOM updates.

# Cross-Cutting Concerns

**Trace Panel (right drawer)**

* Upstream/Lateral/Downstream links, two-hop mini-graph, impact set preview, quick-link creation (drag-drop).

**Performance Budgets**

* P95: primary reads < 1s; heavy views < 2s; impact analysis < 30s (10k neighborhood).
* CAD viewer initial render < 2s for medium assemblies (lightweight JT/glTF).

**Accessibility & Localization**

* Full keyboard nav, ARIA landmarks, captions/alt text on media, focus order validated. ICU formatting, SI units with localized display.

**Security**

* ABAC per view/action; export control tags; watermark & expiry on external views; audit trails for every approval/signature/download.

**Observability**

* OTel web SDK (route, LCP, errors), backend traces, correlation IDs; dashboards for UX perf, errors, usage funnels.

# APIs & Events (snippets)

**Start Review**

```
POST /v1/reviews
{
  "artifactRefs":[{"type":"Requirement","id":"REQ-123"}],
  "checklistTemplateId":"safety-req-v2",
  "approvers":["u:chief-eng","u:compliance-1"],
  "quorum":2,
  "dueAt":"2025-12-01T17:00:00Z"
}
```

**Approve & Sign**

```
POST /v1/reviews/{id}/approve
{
  "signature": {
    "method":"eidas",
    "certificateRef":"cert:abc123",
    "reason":"Meets ASIL-B criteria"
  }
}
```

**Events**

* `ReviewCreated`, `ReviewApproved`, `BaselineCreated`, `DocumentGenerated`, `SupplierPackageSubmitted`, `InterfaceCheckFailed`, `CommentAdded`, `DecisionLogged`.

Awesome—here’s a crisp, build-ready expansion of the **Core Domain (Lifecycle) Services**. For every service you’ll get: purpose, core objects, key APIs, emitted/consumed events, primary workflows, integrations, non-functionals, KPIs, and “done” checks.

# Requirements Service

**Purpose**: Author/manage needs & requirements, interfaces, variants, baselines; exchange via SysML v2/ReqIF.

* **Core objects**: `Need`, `Requirement`, `Interface`, `Constraint`, `Package(SysMLv2)`, `VariantRule`, `Baseline`, `TradeStudy`.
* **APIs**

  * `POST /requirements` (create), `PATCH /requirements/{id}` (change with reason), `POST /baselines`, `POST /imports/reqif`, `POST /packages/sysml`.
  * GraphQL read: coverage/gaps, upstream/downstream links.
* **Events**: `RequirementCreated|Changed|Baselined`, `InterfaceChanged`, `VariantRuleUpdated`, `TradeStudyDecided`.
* **Workflows**: author → link → variant annotate → baseline + e-sign; trade study (alts→score→decision→links).
* **Integrations**: ALM (stories/tests), MBSE, Change, Test, Compliance, PLM (handoff).
* **NFRs**: read P95 ≤ 150 ms; import 10k ReqIF ≤ 10 min; impact precompute ≤ 30 s (10k neighborhood).
* **KPIs**: trace coverage %, orphan reqs, import fidelity %, baseline rebuild success.
* **Done**: changing a req shows effected tests/parts/WIs within 30 s; baseline hash verifies.

---

# MBSE/Architecture Service

**Purpose**: System architecture models & contracts that drive allocation and verification.

* **Core objects**: `Block`, `Function`, `Port`, `InterfaceContract`, `Allocation`, `ParamModel`, `VariantModel`.
* **APIs**: `POST /architecture/blocks`, `POST /contracts`, `POST /allocations`, `GET /interfaces/{id}/conformance`.
* **Events**: `InterfaceContractPublished`, `AllocationChanged`, `ArchitectureBaselined`.
* **Workflows**: define contracts → allocate requirements → check conformance (supplier/self) → baseline.
* **Integrations**: Simulation Orchestrator (parameters), PLM (CAD interfaces), Supplier Portal (checks).
* **NFRs**: contract diff ≤ 1 s; conformance eval for mid-sized assembly ≤ 5 s.
* **KPIs**: % reqs allocated, interface violations rate/time to fix.
* **Done**: broken contract blocks ECO until waiver attached.

---

# Change Management

**Purpose**: Govern ECR/ECO with auto impact and baseline creation.

* **Core objects**: `ECR`, `ECO`, `ChangePackage`, `Effectivity` (date/lot/serial/market), `Approval`.
* **APIs**: `POST /ecr`, `POST /eco`, `POST /eco/{id}/approve`, `GET /impact?artifact=...`.
* **Events**: `ECRCreated`, `ChangeImpactReady`, `ECOApproved`, `BaselineCreated`.
* **Workflows**: propose → auto-impact (graph) → checklist → approvals (DMN) → ECO execution → baseline stamp.
* **Integrations**: Requirements, Part/BOM, Work Instructions, Test, Compliance, PLM.
* **NFRs**: impact set P95 ≤ 30 s; approver action ≤ 200 ms; baseline stamp ≤ 3 s.
* **KPIs**: cycle time ECR→ECO, rework %, approval SLA hit rate.
* **Done**: ECO approval generates signed baseline and pushes deltas to dependent modules.

---

# ALM/Software Service

**Purpose**: Software work, tests, releases, SBOM, quality gates—traceable to requirements.

* **Core objects**: `Epic`, `Story`, `Task`, `Bug`, `TestCase`, `TestRun`, `Build`, `Release`, `SBOM`, `QualityGate`.
* **APIs**: `POST /stories`, `POST /releases`, `POST /quality/check`, `POST /test-results`.
* **Events**: `BuildCompleted`, `ReleaseCreated`, `SBOMPublished`, `QualityGateFailed`.
* **Workflows**: req→story→PR→CI→tests→release→evidence; safety pathways (coverage, code reviews, static analysis).
* **Integrations**: GitHub/GitLab/Jira, Compliance, Requirements, Test.
* **NFRs**: commit→visible results P95 ≤ 5 min; evidence aggregation ≤ 30 s.
* **KPIs**: lead time, change fail rate, coverage %, SBOM freshness.
* **Done**: release cannot be marked “done” unless gates pass and evidence links exist.

# Test & Verification

**Purpose**: Manage test assets, runs, coverage, and verdicts across sim/HIL/manual.

* **Core objects**: `TestPlan`, `TestCase`, `TestProcedure`, `Rig/HIL`, `Run`, `Result`, `CoverageReport`, `FlakeScore`.
* **APIs**: `POST /tests`, `POST /runs`, `POST /results`, `GET /coverage?baseline=...`.
* **Events**: `TestRunCompleted`, `VerificationStatusChanged`, `TestFlakinessUpdated`.
* **Workflows**: plan → author → link to reqs → execute (CI/HIL) → import results → compute coverage → publish V&V matrix.
* **Integrations**: ALM, Simulation, Requirements, Compliance, Ops (for CAPA validation).
* **NFRs**: import 100k results ≤ 5 min; coverage query ≤ 1 s.
* **KPIs**: verification completeness %, flake rate, mean time from fail→fix.
* **Done**: clicking a req shows latest pass/fail and link to evidence file/logs.

# Simulation Orchestrator

**Purpose**: Run & track models (FMU/FMI and others), scenarios, provenance, and comparisons.

* **Core objects**: `Scenario`, `Model`, `FMU`, `Run`, `ParameterSet`, `Toolchain`, `Metric`, `Comparison`.
* **APIs**: `POST /runs`, `GET /runs/{id}`, `POST /models/fmu`, `POST /comparisons`.
* **Events**: `SimulationRunQueued|Started|Completed`, `ScenarioChanged`.
* **Workflows**: select model+scenario → submit run (container) → store inputs/seeds/provenance → compute/compare → link to req/test.
* **Integrations**: MBSE (params), Test (evidence), Supplier (results), CAE tools.
* **NFRs**: run metadata availability ≤ 60 s post-finish; reproducibility checks exact (within tolerance).
* **KPIs**: reproducibility rate, queue wait time, success rate.
* **Done**: re-run with same inputs produces metrics within tolerance and identical hash manifests.

# PLM Bridge Service

**Purpose**: Sync parts/BOM/changes/docs with Teamcenter/Windchill/etc.

* **Core objects**: `PartRef`, `BOMRef`, `ChangeRef`, `DocRef`, `Classifications`.
* **APIs**: `POST /plm/import`, `POST /plm/commands/{CreateECR|PromoteECO}`, `GET /plm/mappings`.
* **Events**: `PartReleased`, `BOMUpdated`, `ECOApproved` (canonicalized).
* **Workflows**: CDC/webhook ingest → map to canonical → publish; outbound commands with idempotency.
* **Integrations**: Part/BOM Service, Change, Work Instructions, Compliance.
* **NFRs**: 100k parts/day; lag P95 ≤ 5 min; BOM 50k lines streaming.
* **KPIs**: sync freshness, mapping coverage, error/DLQ rate.
* **Done**: ECO approval in PLM triggers internal baseline & downstream updates.

# Part/BOM Service

**Purpose**: Authoritative engineering view when PLM is external, or the canonical mirror.

* **Core objects**: `Part`, `EBOM`, `MBOM`, `AltGroup`, `ApprovedVendor`, `Effectivity`.
* **APIs**: `POST /parts`, `POST /boms`, `GET /boms/{id}/diff`, `POST /cost-rollup`.
* **Events**: `PartCreated|Released`, `BOMChanged`, `MBOMEffed`.
* **Workflows**: part create/classify → EBOM author → MBOM align → alternates & AVL → effectivity.
* **Integrations**: PLM Bridge, Work Instructions, Cost & Vendor, Change.
* **NFRs**: BOM diff ≤ 2 s (5k lines); cost roll-up 10k parts ≤ 2 min.
* **KPIs**: MBOM alignment %, AVL completeness, cost accuracy.
* **Done**: MBOM change propagates WI diff and test impact list.

---

# Configuration & Variants

**Purpose**: Feature models, rules, variant resolution, effectivity (market/lot/serial).

* **Core objects**: `FeatureModel`, `Feature`, `Constraint`, `Resolution`, `EffectivityPolicy`.
* **APIs**: `POST /features`, `POST /resolve?context=...`, `POST /effectivity`.
* **Events**: `FeatureModelChanged`, `VariantResolved`, `EffectivityApplied`.
* **Workflows**: define model + constraints → resolve for program/market → stamp effectivity on parts/WIs/tests.
* **Integrations**: Requirements, Part/BOM, Work Instructions, Test, Twins.
* **NFRs**: resolve ≤ 200 ms (100 features); SAT solver warm cache.
* **KPIs**: resolution success rate, mis-configuration incidents.
* **Done**: EU variant adds EMC tests automatically; US unaffected.

---

# Quality & Risk

**Purpose**: FMEA/FTA, control plans, inspections, audit findings.

* **Core objects**: `FMEAItem` (mode/effect/cause/control), `FTAEvent`, `RiskScore`, `ControlPlan`, `Inspection`.
* **APIs**: `POST /fmea`, `POST /risk/recalc`, `POST /inspections/results`.
* **Events**: `RiskLevelChanged`, `InspectionFailed`, `ControlAdded`.
* **Workflows**: author FMEA → link to design/tests → track mitigations → inspections feed back.
* **Integrations**: Nonconformance/CAPA, Compliance, Ops, Change.
* **NFRs**: risk heatmap render ≤ 1 s; 10k items recompute ≤ 1 min.
* **KPIs**: high-risk count trend, mitigation lead time, inspection pass rate.
* **Done**: raising risk auto-adds checklist items to ECO review.

---

# Nonconformance & CAPA

**Purpose**: Handle NCRs from shop/field; drive CAPA to closure.

* **Core objects**: `NCR`, `Containment`, `RootCause`, `CAPA`, `Verification`.
* **APIs**: `POST /ncr`, `POST /capa`, `PATCH /capa/{id}/status`, `GET /sla`.
* **Events**: `NCRCreated`, `CAPAStarted|Closed`, `VerificationPassed`.
* **Workflows**: detect → NCR → containment → root cause → corrective/preventive → verify with tests/SPC.
* **Integrations**: Ops (alarms/SPC), Change, Test, Work Instructions, Quality.
* **NFRs**: detection→CAPA open < 4 h; SLA timers accurate to minutes.
* **KPIs**: CAPA cycle time, recurrence rate, verification escape rate.
* **Done**: closing CAPA requires linked verification evidence.

---

# Compliance Workbench

**Purpose**: Map standards, manage evidence templates, signoff gates, and packs.

* **Core objects**: `Standard`, `Control`, `EvidenceTemplate`, `Gate`, `EvidencePack`.
* **APIs**: `POST /templates`, `POST /packs/generate`, `POST /gates/check`.
* **Events**: `EvidencePackGenerated`, `GatePassed|Failed`.
* **Workflows**: choose standard → generate evidence from graph → sign → archive with baseline hash.
* **Integrations**: Requirements, Test, Change, ALM, Quality.
* **NFRs**: pack gen P95 ≤ 2 min; verifier CLI ≤ 2 s.
* **KPIs**: audit findings, pack freshness, gate pass rate.
* **Done**: auditor can verify pack via CLI (hash & signatures OK).

---

# Work Instructions

**Purpose**: Author, publish, and sign off station instructions tied to MBOM/effectivity.

* **Core objects**: `WorkInstruction`, `Operation`, `Routing`, `Station`, `Signoff`.
* **APIs**: `POST /wis`, `POST /publish?effectivity=...`, `GET /resolve?station=...`.
* **Events**: `WorkInstructionPublished`, `StationSignedOff`.
* **Workflows**: author → link MBOM & spec values → publish to stations → collect signoffs → track conformance.
* **Integrations**: Part/BOM, Ops/MES, Change, Twins.
* **NFRs**: station resolve P95 < 1 s; publish latency < 15 min from ECO.
* **KPIs**: signoff compliance, instruction freshness, rework incidents.
* **Done**: updated spec shows at next job with correct effectivity badge.

---

# Asset Registry

**Purpose**: Authoritative catalog of equipment/lines/assets & maintenance.

* **Core objects**: `Asset`, `Capability`, `Calibration`, `MaintenanceRecord`, `Availability`.
* **APIs**: `POST /assets`, `POST /calibration`, `POST /maintenance`.
* **Events**: `AssetCommissioned|Decommissioned`, `CalibrationDue`, `MaintenanceCompleted`.
* **Workflows**: register → bind telemetry → track calibration/maintenance → feed into CAPA or availability KPIs.
* **Integrations**: Twins, Ops, Work Instructions, Historian.
* **NFRs**: lookups ≤ 50 ms; list 10k assets ≤ 1 s.
* **KPIs**: calibration on-time %, MTBF/MTTR, availability.
* **Done**: asset page shows as-maintained config and upcoming obligations.

---

# Digital Twin Registry

**Purpose**: Twins for product/system/asset/process with lineage & telemetry bindings.

* **Core objects**: `Twin(kind)`, `Binding`, `ConfigSnapshot(asDesigned|asBuilt|asMaintained)`, `KPI`.
* **APIs**: `POST /twins`, `POST /twins/{id}/bind`, `GET /twins/{id}/lineage`, `POST /twins/{id}/snapshot`.
* **Events**: `TwinRegistered`, `TwinConfigChanged`, `TelemetryBound`.
* **Workflows**: register twin on release → bind telemetry → detect drift → trigger CAPA/ECO.
* **Integrations**: Historian/IIoT, Part/BOM, Requirements, Work Instructions, Ops.
* **NFRs**: twin fetch ≤ 200 ms; drift detection batch < 5 min.
* **KPIs**: twin coverage %, drift incidents, mean diagnosis time.
* **Done**: for a serial, show as-maintained vs as-built diff and upstream reqs in < 5 s.

---

# Operations Hub

**Purpose**: Real-time ops dashboards, SPC/OEE, shift reports, NCR triggers.

* **Core objects**: `Alarm`, `SPCSeries`, `OEE`, `ShiftReport`, `OperatorNote`.
* **APIs**: `GET /ops/line/:id`, `POST /ops/note`, `POST /ncr` (quick create).
* **Events**: `AlarmRaised|Cleared`, `ProcessCapabilityChanged`, `OEEUpdated`.
* **Workflows**: monitor → detect anomalies → NCR/CAPA → feedback to engineering.
* **Integrations**: Historian, Work Instructions, Nonconformance, Twins.
* **NFRs**: edge→dashboard P95 < 10 s; line view P95 < 1 s.
* **KPIs**: detection→CAPA open time, SPC violations trend, OEE.
* **Done**: alarm automatically creates NCR with linked context and owner.

---

# Portfolio & Program

**Purpose**: Plan programs/roadmaps, capacity, PI objectives; report EV (SPI/CPI).

* **Core objects**: `Program`, `RoadmapItem`, `Epic`, `Dependency`, `CapacityPlan`, `Milestone`, `EV(PV/EV/AC)`.
* **APIs**: `POST /programs`, `POST /capacity`, `GET /ev`.
* **Events**: `EpicCommitted`, `MilestoneMet`, `BudgetVarianceAlert`.
* **Workflows**: roadmap → dependencies → capacity → PI objectives → monitor EV.
* **Integrations**: ALM, Cost & Vendor, Part/BOM, Compliance (milestone gates).
* **NFRs**: roadmap view ≤ 1 s; EV compute daily.
* **KPIs**: schedule variance, CPI/SPI, dependency slippage.
* **Done**: changing supplier cost updates EV forecasts within 15 min.

---

# Cost & Vendor

**Purpose**: Financials for engineering artifacts; vendor management & scorecards.

* **Core objects**: `CostCenter`, `Vendor`, `PO`, `MaterialCost`, `Quote`, `Scorecard`.
* **APIs**: `POST /vendors`, `POST /cost/material`, `GET /rollup?bom=...`, `POST /scorecards`.
* **Events**: `MaterialCostChanged`, `POReceived`, `VendorScoreUpdated`.
* **Workflows**: ingest costs (ERP) → roll-up → flag variances → vendor performance tracked.
* **Integrations**: ERP, Part/BOM, Portfolio, Supplier Portal.
* **NFRs**: cost roll-up 10k BOM ≤ 2 min; delta updates under 5 min.
* **KPIs**: cost variance, on-time delivery, quality incidents per vendor.
* **Done**: MBOM change or cost update reflects in portfolio risk widgets automatically.

---

## Cross-cutting conventions (applies to all)

* **AuthZ**: ABAC (project, classification, export control, tenant).
* **Events**: canonical Avro/Protobuf, SemVer, outbox pattern, idempotent consumers.
* **Observability**: OTel traces/metrics/logs; per-service SLOs and dashboards.
* **Data**: Postgres OLTP; OpenSearch projections; Graph sidecar for links; Iceberg for analytics.
* **Docs**: OpenAPI/AsyncAPI, runbooks, user guides; examples/golden payloads included.

Awesome—here’s a “ship-ready” playbook for **Integration & Connectors**. For each bridge family you’ll get: scope, auth, contracts, flows (inbound/outbound), mappings, error handling, SLOs, observability, security, and acceptance tests. Cross-cutting scaffolds are first so every team builds the same way.

---

# Cross-cutting blueprint (applies to all connectors)

**Runtime pattern**

* Each connector = isolated K8s Deployment + Outbox table + Kafka producer.
* Inbound: Webhooks / polling / CDC → **canonical events** (`int.{system}.cdc.*`) → transform → `dom.*` events.
* Outbound: REST/gRPC commands with retries, **idempotency keys**, and circuit breakers.

**Contracts & versioning**

* OpenAPI for commands; AsyncAPI for events; Avro/Protobuf schemas in `contracts/`.
* SemVer with **backward-compatible** MINOR/PATCH; MAJOR requires deprecation plan.

**Reliability**

* Retries (3–5 w/ jitter), DLQ per stream, replay by time/offset, poison-pill quarantine.
* Idempotency key = `sourceSystemId + externalId + operation + digest(payload)`.

**Observability**

* OTel traces (webhook → transform → publish/command), metrics: `events_processed_total`, `lag_ms`, `retry_total`, `dlq_depth`, `map_error_total`, `rate_limit_hits_total`.
* Logs JSON with `trace_id`, `tenant`, `external_id`, `op`.

**Security**

* OAuth 2.0 / PAT rotation via Vault; IP allowlists; outgoing egress allowlisted.
* PII redaction; export-controlled fields masked; watermarking for files; audit stream for all writes.

**SLOs (default)**

* Status reflected in UI ≤ **60 s** P95 (ALM/SCM/PLM).
* Edge→dashboard ≤ **10 s** P95 (IIoT).
* DLQ drained < **24 h**.

**Acceptance (common)**

* Golden dataset replays to green; replays are idempotent; DLQ < threshold; dashboards show zero mapping errors.

---

## 1) ALM Bridges — Jira / Azure DevOps

**Scope**

* Epics/issues/tests/runs; comments; attachments metadata; workflows.

**Auth**

* Jira Cloud OAuth app / ADO OAuth (or PATs for on-prem). Rotate 90d.

**Inbound (ALM → Platform)**

* Webhooks: `issue_updated`, `worklog_updated`, `test_run_completed` (ADO).
* Transform → `dom.alm.issue.changed`, `dom.test.run.completed`.

**Outbound (Platform → ALM)**

* Create/update issues/tests; transition states; attach links.
* Endpoint examples:

  * `POST /alm/{tenant}/jira/issues` → creates Story + back-link to Requirement.
  * `POST /alm/{tenant}/ado/tests/results` → bulk import.

**Field mapping (sample)**

| Platform           | Jira/ADO                         | Notes                      |
| ------------------ | -------------------------------- | -------------------------- |
| Requirement.id     | Issue.customfield_requirement_id | 1:1 link                   |
| Story.state        | Issue.status                     | Transition map per project |
| TestCase.id        | ADO TestCase ID                  | Preserve external key      |
| VerificationStatus | Jira Status/Resolution           | Derived mapping            |

**Edge cases**

* Custom workflows: per-project transition map YAML.
* Attachments: store SHA-256; lazy fetch via signed proxy URL.
* Bulk throttling: 10 rps/project; exponential backoff on HTTP 429.

**SLO**

* Issue status change visible ≤ 60 s P95.

**Acceptance**

* Change a Story to “Done” → Requirement verification badge updates and V&V matrix reflects within 60 s.

---

## 2) SCM/CI Bridges — GitHub / GitLab / Azure Repos

**Scope**

* Commits, PR/MR, CI builds, test reports (xUnit/JUnit), coverage, artifacts, code scanning, releases, SBOM.

**Auth**

* GitHub App / GitLab App; granular repo scopes.

**Inbound**

* Webhooks: `push`, `check_suite.completed`, `workflow_job.completed`, `release.published`, `code_scanning.alert`.
* Parse → `dom.ci.build.completed`, `dom.test.run.completed`, `dom.release.created`, `dom.vuln.detected`.

**Outbound**

* Post status checks to PR/MR (“Evidence completeness”, “Trace links present”) with deep links.

**Artifact ingestion**

* Pull artifacts to object store (range requests), save digest; publish `ArtifactIngested`.

**Quality gates**

* Coverage ≥ X, vuln severity ≤ Y, required reviewers ≥ Z → gate release creation.

**SLO**

* Commit→results visible P95 ≤ 5 min.

**Acceptance**

* Tag a release → SBOM + provenance ingested, release blocked if gate fails; unblock after fixing and re-run.

---

## 3) PLM/PDM Bridges — Teamcenter / Windchill / 3DEXPERIENCE

**Scope**

* Parts, EBOM/MBOM, documents (metadata + lightweight renders), change objects (ECR/ECO), classifications.

**Auth**

* SSO + app certificate / OAuth via gateway; IP allowlists.

**Inbound**

* CDC or vendor webhooks → `PartReleased`, `BOMUpdated`, `ECOApproved`. Stream large BOMs incrementally (paged, checkpointed).

**Outbound**

* `CreateECR`, `AttachAffectedItems`, `PromoteECO`, `GetJT` (lightweight).
* Idempotency via external change number.

**Mappings**

* `{partNo, rev, lifecycle, class, uom, mass, material}`, BOM lines `{parent, child, qty, findNo, altGroup, effectivity}`.

**Files**

* Store renders (JT/glTF) only for externals; watermark upon view.

**SLO**

* Lag P95 ≤ 5 min for part/BOM changes; ECO approval reflected ≤ 2 min.

**Acceptance**

* Approve ECO in PLM → MBOM/WI/test impact list updated; signed baseline created automatically.

---

## 4) ERP Bridges — SAP / Oracle

**Scope**

* Material cost, POs, vendor master; release handoffs (optional write).

**Auth**

* SAP BTP / Oracle IDCS OAuth; client credentials.

**Inbound**

* Cost tables nightly + deltas via CDC; PO receipts near-real-time.
* Publish `MaterialCostChanged`, `POReceived`, `VendorChanged`.

**Outbound**

* `ReleaseToManufacture` → create/update IDoc/ODATA, idempotent key = baselineId.

**Data rules**

* Currency normalized (FX rate recorded); multi-plant cost resolution; cost roll-up on MBOM change.

**SLO**

* Cost delta → portfolio forecast update ≤ 15 min.

**Acceptance**

* Update material cost in SAP → roll-up shows new program forecast & risk badge change inside 15 min.

---

## 5) MES/MOM Bridges — Opcenter / Ignition / Others

**Scope**

* Publish Work Instructions, capture station signoffs, SPC feeds, alarms.

**Auth**

* API keys/OAuth; station tokens (short-lived).

**Outbound**

* `POST /mes/work-instructions/publish` with effectivity/baseline; push deltas only.

**Inbound**

* Signoffs, SPC series, alarms → `StationSignedOff`, `SPCUpdated`, `AlarmRaised`.

**Offline/edge**

* Queue at site; reconciliation with dedupe when back online.

**SLO**

* ECO→new WI visible at station ≤ 15 min; alarm→NCR create ≤ 60 s.

**Acceptance**

* Torque spec change → new WI at station next job; signoff stored with correct effectivity & baseline ID.

---

## 6) CAE/CAD Bridges — Ansys / Simcenter / Viewers

**Scope**

* Job orchestration metadata, results, and viewer streaming; CAD metadata ingest.

**Auth**

* Service accounts + MTLS; viewer tokens scoped (no raw CAD export for externals).

**Inbound**

* `SimulationRunCompleted` with manifest (inputs, toolchain, metrics, digests).
* CAD metadata (BOM, attributes) + lightweight render (JT/glTF) for viewers.

**Outbound**

* Job submit (container image + inputs) to CAE farm; status poll or webhook.

**SLO**

* Run metadata visible ≤ 60 s post-finish; viewer open ≤ 2 s for medium models.

**Acceptance**

* Re-run same job → identical metrics within tolerance; viewer watermark + redaction enforced for suppliers.

---

## 7) Math/Modeling Bridges — MATLAB/Simulink, Modelica, FMU

**Scope**

* FMU packaging, parameter handoff, model validation, code-gen metadata.

**Inbound**

* Model export notifications; parameter dictionaries; code-gen reports.

**Outbound**

* Export/pack FMUs with IO contracts; push parameter sets to orchestrator.

**Toolchain provenance**

* Capture versions, licenses, hashes; sign manifests.

**SLO**

* FMU pack within 2 min for typical models; parameter sync < 10 s.

**Acceptance**

* Change parameter set → orchestrator run uses new values; manifest shows provenance & diff.

---

## 8) Historian/IIoT Bridges — OPC UA, MQTT Sparkplug B, PI/Ignition

**Scope**

* Telemetry ingest, unit normalization, late/out-of-order handling, alarms.

**Auth**

* X.509 on edge; broker mutual TLS; token per site.

**Inbound**

* OPC UA clients / MQTT Sparkplug → Kafka ingest; Historian APIs/CDC for backfill.
* Flink jobs: normalize units (UCUM), quality flags, compress (Gorilla), rollups.

**Late data**

* Watermarks + reorder buffer; merge into Iceberg; emit `RecomputedMetric` on KPI changes.

**SLO**

* Edge→hot store ≤ 10 s P95; late data reconciliation < 15 min.

**Acceptance**

* Backfill a day of temps → SPC recalculates; dashboards & NCR analytics update automatically.

---

## 9) Directory/Identity — OIDC/SAML/SCIM

**Scope**

* Tenant onboarding, SSO, SCIM provisioning (users/groups), policy sync.

**Inbound**

* SCIM `POST/PUT` users/groups → internal directory; `UserProvisioned`, `RoleChanged`.

**Outbound**

* Policy claims to external IdP (optional); group suggestions.

**SLO**

* User provisioned and able to log in ≤ 5 min.

**Acceptance**

* Add user to “Approvers” in IdP → can approve within 5 min; “why denied” tool explains ABAC failures.

---

## 10) Notifications & Chat — Email / Slack / Teams

**Scope**

* Mentions, reviews, approvals, KPI alerts; action links (deep links with context).

**Outbound**

* Webhooks to Slack/Teams; SMTP/API for email; digest jobs.

**Inbound**

* Slash commands/webhooks to act on items (approve, comment) with scoped tokens.

**Formatting**

* Short actionable cards; include artifact type/id/state; avoid PII.

**SLO**

* Page or critical approval → message < 30 s; digests at user-config times.

**Acceptance**

* Approve from Slack card updates review & writes signature; audit trail includes channel + actor.

---

# Security & Compliance hardening (all connectors)

* **Zero trust**: mTLS everywhere; JWT audience checks; token rotation alarms.
* **DLP**: redact sensitive fields; outbound allowlist; attachment scanning.
* **Tamper-evidence**: sign change payloads (DSSE) when writing to third parties.
* **Audit**: immutable logs of all connector actions; OPA decision logs shipped to SIEM.

---

# Cost & Performance controls

* Rate-limiters per tenant and per integration.
* Backpressure: bounded queues; degrade gracefully (drop non-critical enrichments first).
* Cardinality budgets for metrics; log sampling for INFO.

---

# Testing & certification

**Contract tests**

* Provider/consumer Pact for REST; AsyncAPI simulators for events; golden payload sets per system/version.

**Soak tests**

* 1–7 day runs at expected peak rates; measure lag, error, DLQ.

**Chaos**

* Simulate webhook outages, 429 storms, malformed payloads, id changes; verify idempotency and no data loss.

---

# Ops runbooks (example snippets)

**“429 rate limit from Jira”**

* Symptoms: rising `rate_limit_hits_total`, lag growth.
* Actions: Raise backoff, enable batch mode, schedule catch-up window, notify project owners.

**“PLM BOM stream stuck”**

* Check checkpoint offsets; compare vendor API health; switch to paged fetch; re-seed from last good changeId.

**“MQTT burst from site”**

* Verify broker; scale Flink operators; drop to high-priority tags only; notify OT.

---

# Rollout plan (first 3 PIs)

* **PI-1:** ALM + SCM/CI + basic PLM import; Notifications; Identity.
* **PI-2:** PLM write-backs; ERP cost; MES WI publish + signoff; Historian ingest v1.
* **PI-3:** CAE/Math FMU flow; Supplier checks; late-data reconciliation; Slack/Teams action cards.

---

# KPIs (integration health)

* Freshness (median; P95) per connector.
* Error rate < 0.1%; DLQ depth < threshold w/ 24h drain.
* Idempotency violations = 0; duplicate suppression rate > 99.99%.
* Partner app satisfaction (NPS), time to onboard (< 48 h).

Amazing—here’s a concrete, build-ready blueprint for **Data & Analytics**. I’ve broken it down by subsystem with: architecture, schemas/contracts, pipelines, governance/quality, APIs/queries, SLOs/cost controls, security, KPIs, and acceptance tests. Copy/paste friendly.

---

# 1) Operational Datastores

**Purpose:** Low-latency OLTP per service; hot telemetry for ops/analytics.

## 1.1 Postgres per service (OLTP)

* **Pattern:** schema-per-service; strict ownership; CQRS (read projections separate).
* **Migrations:** Flyway/Liquibase; forward-only; blue/green with shadow writes.
* **Recommended extensions:** `pg_partman` (time/hash); `pgcrypto`; `uuid-ossp`.
* **Backups/HA:** Patroni HA; WAL archiving to object store; PITR enabled.
* **Indices:** partial indexes for active rows; `btree` on FKs; GIN for tags/JSONB.

**Example (Change service)**

```sql
CREATE TABLE eco (
  eco_id        TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
  state         TEXT NOT NULL,
  effectivity   JSONB,
  baseline_id   TEXT,
  created_at    TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
  updated_at    TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL
);
CREATE INDEX eco_state_idx ON eco(state);
```

**SLOs:** p95 single-row read ≤ 20 ms (in-region); p95 write ≤ 30 ms.

---

## 1.2 Timeseries DB (Timescale or VictoriaMetrics)

* **Use:** IIoT process data, SPC/OEE, alarms, job metrics.
* **Ingest:** Kafka → Flink normalizer (unit conversion, quality flags, late/out-of-order handling).
* **Retention tiers:** 90d hot (1–10s resolution), 1–2y warm (1m/15m rollups), cold in Lakehouse.
* **Compression:** Timescale native or Gorilla; downsampled continuous aggregates.

**Canonical measurement**

```json
{
  "ts":"2025-11-04T12:00:00.000Z",
  "tenant":"t1",
  "site":"munich",
  "assetId":"press-42",
  "signal":"torque",
  "value":54.2,
  "uom":"N·m",
  "quality":"good",
  "source":"sparkplug",
  "labels":{"station":"S07","job":"J12345"}
}
```

**SLOs:** edge→queryable P95 < 10 s; write success ≥ 99.999%.

---

# 2) Lakehouse

**Purpose:** Durable, scalable analytics store for “one-truth” reporting, ML, and audits.

## 2.1 Storage & table formats

* **Format:** Apache Iceberg (or Delta Lake) on S3-compatible object storage.
* **Partitioning:** by `{tenant}/{domain}/{yyyy}/{MM}/{dd}`; further by hour for high volume.
* **Sorting/Z-order:** on high-selectivity columns (`assetId`, `signal`, `aggregateId`).
* **Compaction:** small file compaction nightly; clustering weekly; vacuum with retention.

**Core tables (illustrative)**

* `req_events` (schema-on-write from canonical events)
* `eco_events`, `bom_snapshots`, `test_results`, `simulation_runs`,
* `telemetry_1s`, `telemetry_1m`, `kpi_facts_daily`, `cost_rollups_monthly`.

## 2.2 Compute

* **Ad-hoc/BI:** Trino.
* **Batch/ETL:** Spark (structured streaming for near-real-time KPIs).
* **Scheduling:** Airflow or Argo Workflows with git-versioned DAGs.

## 2.3 Ingest patterns

* **Events:** Kafka → Flink → Iceberg append; exactly-once sinks with transactional writers.
* **DB CDC:** Debezium → Kafka → Spark merge into Iceberg (upserts).
* **Backfills:** bounded replays with watermarking; idempotent merge semantics (natural keys + `version`).

## 2.4 Governance & lineage

* **Catalog:** Apache Atlas or Amundsen (table/column lineage, owners, glossary).
* **Lineage sources:** Spark/Trino hooks + event schemas; visual graphs in Atlas UI.
* **Stewardship:** data owners per domain; stewards per curated marts.

**SLOs:** event→Iceberg visibility P95 < 5 min; Trino P95 interactive query < 10 s (star schema marts).

---

# 3) Knowledge / Ontology

**Purpose:** Shared semantics for cross-domain reasoning and doc generation.

## 3.1 Models

* **RDF/OWL** (preferred for interoperability) or **Labeled Property Graph (LPG)** overlaying the trace graph.
* **Vocabulary:** `omni:` namespace for core classes (`Requirement`, `Part`, `TestCase`, `Twin`, `Baseline`, `EvidencePack`).
* **Mappings:** ReqIF ↔ `omni:Requirement`; SysML v2 elements ↔ `omni:Block`/`omni:Interface`; STEP/JT ↔ `omni:DesignItem`.

## 3.2 Constraints

* **SHACL** shapes to enforce business rules (e.g., every `SafetyRequirement` **must** have ≥1 `verifies` link from a `TestCase` before `Released`).
* **Validation:** nightly graph validation job; violations to “Data Quality” board.

**Example SHACL snippet**

```turtle
omni:SafetyRequirementShape a sh:NodeShape ;
  sh:targetClass omni:SafetyRequirement ;
  sh:property [
    sh:path omni:verifiedBy ;
    sh:minCount 1 ;
  ] .
```

**SLO:** ontology load < 3 s; validation of 1M triples < 15 min.

---

# 4) Analytics Packs

**Purpose:** Out-of-the-box, governed metrics for engineering lifecycle, quality/reliability, and cost/schedule risk.

## 4.1 Lifecycle KPIs (precise definitions)

* **Lead time for change (software):** median time from first commit on a PR → production deployment timestamp.
* **Change cycle time (ECR→ECO approved):** P90 time from `ECRCreated.occurredAt` → `ECOApproved.occurredAt`.
* **Rework rate:** ECOs with `reason ∈ {DEFECT, ESCAPE, NCR}` / total ECOs.
* **Defect escape rate:** defects detected in Verify/Operate after release / total defects for that release.
* **MTTApprove:** mean from `ApprovalRequested` → last required `ApprovalGranted`.

**Trino examples**

```sql
-- Change cycle time (days)
SELECT percentile(cast(date_diff('day', ecr.ts, eco.ts) AS DOUBLE), 0.9) AS p90_days
FROM kf.eco_events eco
JOIN kf.ecr_events ecr ON eco.ecr_id = ecr.ecr_id
WHERE ecr.ts >= date_add('month', -1, current_date);

-- Rework rate (monthly)
SELECT
  sum(CASE WHEN eco.reason IN ('DEFECT','ESCAPE','NCR') THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) / count(*) AS rework_rate
FROM kf.eco_events eco
WHERE eco.ts BETWEEN date_trunc('month', current_date) AND current_date;
```

## 4.2 Reliability & Quality

* **SPC (Cp/Cpk)** by process/characteristic; **FRACAS** trends; **flakiness index** for test cases.
* **Analytics outputs:** `spc_capability_daily`, `flake_scores`, `ncr_capa_flow`.

## 4.3 Cost/Schedule Risk

* **Earned Value (EV):** SPI/CPI from ALM/ERP combo.
* **Forecasting:** Monte Carlo on velocity + risk burn; P50/P90 dates.
* **Variances:** material cost deltas from ERP vs MBOM roll-ups.

**Spark job sketch**

* Join `cost_rollups_monthly` with ERP `material_cost_delta` → compute `variance_pct` → flag >±5%.

**SLO:** daily marts refresh by 06:00 local; KPI freshness < 15 min for near-real-time boards where applicable.

---

# 5) Feature Store (optional)

**Purpose:** Reusable, governed features for ML (predictive quality, anomaly detection, ETA, risk).

## 5.1 Tech & layout

* **Store:** Feast or custom on Iceberg + Redis/VM for online.
* **Registry:** feature definitions (SQL/UDFs), owners, training/serving schemas, backfills.

**Examples**

* `proc_mean_15m(assetId, signal)`; `spc_violation_rate_24h(station)`; `eco_rework_probability_features(program, component)`.

**Materialization**

* Offline: Spark jobs write to Iceberg `features_*`.
* Online: KStreams/Flink push to Redis keyed by entity id.

**Governance**

* Drift monitors; backtest notebooks; approvals for new features (privacy review).

**SLOs:** online TTL < 5 s from source event; offline availability by 06:00 daily.

---

# 6) Dashboard Service (Grafana-as-code)

**Purpose:** Product, SRE, exec, and audit dashboards, versioned alongside code.

## 6.1 Structure

```
dashboards/
  product/verify_coverage.json
  quality/spc_oee_overview.json
  exec/portfolio_health.json
  sre/service_slos.json
  audit/evidence_freshness.json
alerts/
  slo_burn.rules.yml
  kpi_thresholds.rules.yml
```

**Provisioning**

* Grafana Operator/Provisioners; Alertmanager routes; folders with RBAC (audit read-only).

**Templates**

* Variables: tenant, program, product, component, baseline.
* Links: deep-link back to artifact pages and graph impact views.

**SLOs:** board load P95 < 2 s; query budgets per panel < 1 s (cache for heavy).

---

# 7) Data Contracts & Quality

**Contracts**

* **Event schemas:** Avro/Protobuf with SemVer compatibility gates.
* **Table schemas:** Iceberg with column descriptions, classification tags.

**Quality SLAs**

* **Freshness:** event→projection < 60 s P95; event→lakehouse < 5 min P95.
* **Completeness:** required fields ≥ 99.5% by class (safety higher).
* **Validity:** schema/SHACL pass ≥ 99.9%.
* **Uniqueness:** no duplicate business keys; dedupe rate tracked.

**DQ tooling**

* Great Expectations/Deequ suites in CI & scheduled ETL jobs; violations → DLQ/quarantine tables + Slack tickets.

---

# 8) Security & Privacy

* **Classification:** column-level tags (internal/confidential/export_controlled).
* **Row-level filters:** Trino/Iceberg row filters by tenant/project via ABAC.
* **Encryption:** SSE at rest; envelope encryption for sensitive columns (KMS).
* **PII minimization:** telemetry/ML pipelines scrub or hash.
* **Audit:** data access logs shipped to SIEM; “who queried what” reports.

---

# 9) Cost & Performance Controls

* **Storage:** small file compaction; snapshot expiry; cold tiering beyond N months.
* **Compute:** Trino resource groups; query timeouts; cached extracts for popular boards.
* **Telemetry:** tail-sampling on traces; log retention tiers; metric label cardinality budgets.
* **Auto-tuning:** adaptive parallelism for Spark; dynamic partition pruning.

---

# 10) APIs & Access Patterns

* **SQL:** Trino endpoint for analysts/BI.
* **REST (read):** `/analytics/kpi/:name?from=...&to=...&tenant=...` → JSON.
* **GraphQL (read):** consolidated KPI service for UI.
* **CLI:** `omni kpi run --pack lifecycle --from -30d`, `omni lake compact --table telemetry_1s`.

---

# 11) KPIs (Data Platform Health)

* Freshness (proj & lake); DQ pass rate; schema compat failures; Iceberg small-file ratio; Trino success rate/latency; feature staleness; dashboard error rate.

---

# 12) Acceptance Tests (end-to-end)

1. **Trace→KPI:** Update Jira issue to “Done” → `VerificationStatusChanged` event → V&V coverage dashboard updates within 15 min; Trino query returns new percentage.
2. **Late data:** Backfill historian day; SPC metrics recompute; `RecomputedMetric` event emitted; Ops board updates automatically.
3. **Baseline evidence rebuild:** Generate evidence pack from baseline B; delete materialized pack; rebuild solely from Lakehouse/Graph → hashes match.
4. **Ontology/SHACL:** Introduce a safety requirement without verifying test → SHACL job flags violation; Compliance gate blocks release.
5. **Row-level security:** Analyst from tenant A querying tenant B data gets 0 rows; audit log shows deny reasons.

---

# 13) Rollout Plan (3 PIs)

* **PI-1:** Lakehouse bootstrap (Iceberg/Trino), events ingest for req/change/test, Timeseries hot path, Atlas/Amundsen, lifecycle KPIs v1, dashboards-as-code.
* **PI-2:** ERP cost marts, SPC/OEE marts, ontology + SHACL, DQ pipeline, feature store offline, exec dashboards.
* **PI-3:** Online feature store, predictive quality MVP, advanced EV/risk packs, late-data reconciliation, cost guardrails & compaction automation.

Awesome—here’s a complete, “ready-to-ship” blueprint for **Marketplace & Extensibility**. It’s opinionated and concrete so product, platform, security, and partner teams can build in parallel.

---

# 0) Principles (guardrails)

* **Extensibility without fragility**: strict contracts, stable surfaces, clear versioning.
* **Least privilege**: explicit permissions, short-lived scoped tokens, auditable actions.
* **Ecosystem quality**: certification gates (security/perf/a11y/contracts) before publish.
* **Observability & billing by design**: every extension emits OTel and metering events.
* **Upgrades are boring**: compatibility registry, auto canary, rollback.

---

# 1) SDKs

## 1.1 UI Micro-Frontend (MFE) SDK

* **Host model**: React shell with Module Federation; MFEs load at runtime.
* **Exports required**:

  * `register()` → declares routes, panels, command-palette items.
  * `mount(node, ctx)` / `unmount()`; `ctx` gives GraphQL client, i18n, feature flags, telemetry.
* **Manifest (`extension.json`)**

  ```json
  {
    "name": "cfd-viewer",
    "version": "1.3.0",
    "type": "ui",
    "routes": [
      {"path": "/part/:id/cfd", "mount": "Panel", "title": "CFD", "icon": "waves"}
    ],
    "permissions": ["read:part", "read:simulationResult", "subscribe:event:SimulationRunCompleted"],
    "scopes": ["tenant:read"],
    "telemetry": {"otlp": "required"},
    "localization": ["en","de","fr"],
    "compatibility": {"platform": ">=1.8.0 <2.0.0"}
  }
  ```
* **UI APIs**:

  * `useGraphQL(query, vars)`, `useEvent(topic, filter)`, `usePolicy(resource, action)`,
  * `openPanel(route, params)`, `notify({kind, message, action})`,
  * `trace.startSpan(name)`, `metrics.increment(name, tags)` (proxied to OTel).
* **UX requirements**: a11y (WCAG AA), i18n hooks, route budgets (<250KB gz/route), dark mode support, keyboard shortcuts.

## 1.2 Server Plugin SDK (gRPC/REST)

* **Runtime**: out-of-process sidecar (container) with sandbox network policies.
* **Interface** (gRPC primary):

  ```proto
  service Extension {
    rpc Capabilities(Empty) returns (CapabilitiesReply);
    rpc Execute(ExecuteRequest) returns (ExecuteReply);
    rpc OnEvent(Event) returns (Ack);
  }
  message ExecuteRequest { string op = 1; bytes payload = 2; map<string,string> claims = 3; }
  ```
* **HTTP adapter**: OpenAPI scaffold for languages without gRPC.
* **Lifecycles**: health/readiness endpoints; graceful shutdown; backpressure (HTTP 429 / gRPC status RESOURCE_EXHAUSTED).
* **Data access**: no direct DB; call platform BFFs (GraphQL/REST); object access via signed URLs.

## 1.3 Webhooks & Events

* **Subscription model**: AsyncAPI with filters (tenant, type, regex); signed deliveries; replay cursors.
* **Envelope**:

  ```json
  { "id":"ULID", "type":"ChangeApproved", "tenant":"t1",
    "occurredAt":"2025-11-05T10:20:00Z", "schema":"2.1.0", "data":{...}, "sig":"dsse:..." }
  ```
* **Reliability**: at-least-once, idempotency keys, exponential backoff, DLQ with self-serve retries.

## 1.4 Model Transformers

* **Purpose**: convert external artifacts into canonical (e.g., STEP→Part/BOM; ReqIF↔Requirement; FMU packager).
* **Interface**:

  * Input: object IDs or streams + mapping profile.
  * Output: canonical JSON + evidence (digests, warnings).
* **Validation**: SHACL/JSON-Schema; produce `TransformReport` with counters and sample errors.

## 1.5 Schema Adapters

* **Mapping DSL** (YAML):

  ```yaml
  maps:
    - from: jira.issue.fields.priority
      to: requirement.priority
      transform: lookup(priority_map)
    - from: doors.object.text
      to: requirement.text
      transform: sanitize_md()
  ```
* **Contract tests**: golden payloads; must pass on CI before publish.

## 1.6 Tooling & CLI

* `omni ext init` (scaffold), `omni ext dev` (local shell), `omni ext test` (contract tests),
  `omni ext pack` (SBOM + provenance), `omni ext publish` (portal), `omni ext certify` (runs pipeline).

---

# 2) Extension Runtime

## 2.1 Isolation & Security

* **UI**: iframe sandbox + MF host boundary; CSP locked; postMessage bridge with allowlisted API.
* **Server plugins**: dedicated K8s namespace, network policies, resource quotas, read-only root FS, seccomp/AppArmor, non-root UID.
* **Secrets**: short-lived JWT with scopes; Vault broker for long-lived credentials forbidden.

## 2.2 Permissions & Tokens

* Permission strings `verb:resource` (`read:part`, `write:change`, `subscribe:event:*`).
* Tokens: JWT (15–60 min), audience = `omni-api`, bound to tenant & extension id; refresh by host only.

## 2.3 Rate limits & Quotas

* Per-tenant/per-extension limits for: API calls, events, compute (CPU/GB-min), storage/egress.
* Burst + sustained buckets; headers expose remaining quota.

## 2.4 Observability

* **Required**: OTel traces/metrics/logs; `extension`, `version`, `tenant` labels.
* Default dashboards: latency, errors, RUM (for MFEs), resource usage, quota consumption.

## 2.5 Lifecycle

* Install → grant permissions → provision secrets/queues → canary cohort (5%) → full rollout → auto rollback on SLO breach.
* Uninstall → revoke tokens → clean queues/projections → scrub PII.

---

# 3) Partner Portal

## 3.1 Onboarding

* Company profile, legal (DPA, export-control), publisher key, revenue info.
* Pick **sandbox tenants** (EU/US regions), seed datasets (“steel thread” project, IIoT demo).

## 3.2 Docs & Samples

* **“Hello World”** MFE & plugin; full connector examples (Jira, Teamcenter, MQTT).
* AsyncAPI/OpenAPI catalogs, event simulators, golden datasets.

## 3.3 Dev/Test Sandboxes

* Isolated environments with:

  * event simulator (replay canonical events),
  * mock PLM/ERP endpoints,
  * preloaded artifacts (BOMs, tests, CAPA cases),
  * fake IIoT stream generator.

## 3.4 Publishing Workflow

* Submit → automated certification → human UX/security spot check (high risk only) → staged release to selected tenants → GA.

---

# 4) Certification Service

## 4.1 Pipeline Stages

1. **Static checks**: manifest schema, permission rationale, size budgets, CSP compliance.
2. **Security**: SAST/DAST, SBOM (CycloneDX), vuln scan (no criticals), container scan.
3. **Performance**:

   * UI: boot P95 ≤ 500 ms, route P95 ≤ 1 s; memory < 100 MB.
   * Server: p95 latency < 200 ms (typical ops), error rate < 0.5%.
4. **Accessibility (UI)**: axe-core pass, keyboard nav, contrast ≥ AA.
5. **Contract tests**: run against golden events/APIs; idempotency verified.
6. **Observability**: OTel signals present; PII scrubbed; log volume within budgets.
7. **Security review**: permission scope justification; data residency flags.
8. **Live canary**: 24–72 h on internal tenant.

**Outcome**: badge (Bronze/Silver/Gold); expiry 12 months; failing checks block publish.

## 4.2 Version Compatibility Registry

* Matrix: platform version ↔ extension version; deprecation windows; auto-notify publishers of breaking changes.

## 4.3 Breakage Response

* Automated impact analysis → targeted emails & portal alerts → safe-mode disable (if critical) with rollback instructions.

---

# 5) Billing & Licensing

## 5.1 Metering Signals

* **Events** consumed/produced (per topic family).
* **MAU**: distinct active users per tenant using the extension.
* **Compute**: CPU-min/GB-min for server plugins; storage bytes; egress GB.
* **Premium APIs**: count per endpoint (if applicable).

All emitted as signed `BillingUsage` events hourly.

## 5.2 Plans

* **Free** (caps), **Pro** (higher caps + support), **Enterprise** (SLA, private regions).
* Pricing knobs: per MAU, per million events, per compute hour, per GB storage/egress.

## 5.3 Invoicing Hooks

* Monthly aggregation → webhook to billing system (e.g., Stripe, NetSuite) with signed payload; dispute window; credit notes.

## 5.4 Licensing

* Cloud: keyless (publisher id + tenant grants).
* Air-gapped: license file signed; usage beacons cached & exportable.

## 5.5 Revenue Share

* Net receipts minus payment fees; monthly payout; transparent reporting in portal.

---

# 6) APIs (selected)

* **Install**

  ```
  POST /v1/marketplace/extensions/{id}/install
  { "tenant":"t1", "permissions":["read:part","subscribe:event:*"], "plan":"pro" }
  ```
* **Token exchange**

  ```
  POST /v1/marketplace/extensions/{id}/token
  { "tenant":"t1", "scopes":["read:part"] } → { "access_token": "...", "expires_in": 1800 }
  ```
* **Publish**

  ```
  POST /v1/marketplace/publish
  { "bundle":"base64..", "sbom":"...", "provenance":"...", "manifest":{...} }
  ```
* **Certification status**

  ```
  GET /v1/marketplace/certifications/{buildId}
  ```

# 7) Security, Compliance & Legal

* **PII/DLP**: content scanning; export-control flags in manifest; external shares watermarked.
* **Supply chain**: SBOM required; image & artifact signing (Sigstore); provenance attestations.
* **Policies**: forbidden categories (malware, spyware, unsafe code); brand guidelines; support SLAs per plan.
* **Auditing**: immutable logs for installs, permission grants, token mints, API calls.

# 8) Ops: SLOs, KPIs, Alerts

* **SLOs**

  * Extension token mint P95 ≤ 100 ms.
  * Webhook delivery success ≥ 99.9% (rolling 30d).
  * Certification pipeline median < 20 min; P95 < 60 min.
* **KPIs**

  * Time-to-first-hello-world < 1 day.
  * % extensions with Gold badge ≥ 60%.
  * Ecosystem NPS ≥ 60; partner churn < 5%/yr.
  * Crash-free MFE sessions ≥ 99.5%.
* **Alerts**

  * Error rate spikes, quota exhaustion, slow boot/route, OTel missing, token issuance failures.

# 9) Developer Experience (DX)

* **Testing tools**: event player, webhook catcher, contract test harness, perf harness.
* **Docs**: samples in TS/Java/Python/Go; “build a trace panel” tutorial.

4. **Security**

---

You got it — here’s a deeper, nuts-and-bolts expansion of **Documentation** that you can drop straight into your program. It’s opinionated, end-to-end, and covers architecture, workflows, tooling, governance, compliance, and acceptance tests.

---

# 0) Goals & guardrails

* **Always true by construction**: docs generate from contracts, telemetry, and the Digital Thread wherever possible.
* **Docs-as-code**: everything in git, reviewed, versioned, and CI’d like software.
* **One click from product**: in-product “?” deep-links to the exact page for the user’s role, route, and version.
* **Evidence ready**: audit bundles reproducible from baselines; verifier CLI validates signatures and hashes.
* **Inclusive & accessible**: WCAG AA, plain language, localized, examples-first.

---

# 1) Information architecture (sites, sections, repos)

```
docs/
  product/                 # User/admin docs
  developer/               # API, events, SDKs, samples
  integrations/            # Connector guides, field mappings
  architecture/            # C4, ADRs, RFCs, NFRs, topology
  ops/                     # SRE runbooks, SLOs, incident playbooks
  compliance/              # Standards, evidence templates, verifier docs
  marketplace/             # Partner portal, SDK, certification
  style/                   # Voice/tone, word list, components, templates
  media/                   # Approved images, diagrams, GIFs (source)
  mkdocs.yml | docusaurus.config.js
```

**Inside service repos**

* `README.md` (dev setup), `API.md` (quickstart), link back to canonical docs.
* `/contracts` (OpenAPI/AsyncAPI/Avro) — source of truth for generated references.

---

# 2) Source formats & generators

* **Prose**: Markdown/MDX with front-matter metadata.
* **APIs/events**: OpenAPI → Redoc; AsyncAPI → HTML; Avro/Protobuf → reference tables.
* **Diagrams**: Mermaid & PlantUML (rendered in CI); C4 via PlantUML macros.
* **Data cookbooks**: Jupyter/SQL notebooks (rendered static + downloadable).
* **Templates**: Handlebars/Jinja for evidence/reports (same engine the product uses).

---

# 3) Versioning & publishing

* Branches: `main` (next), `release/x.y` (frozen with product).
* **Site versions**: `/v1.8`, `/v1.9`, `/next` with banner explaining status.
* **Pinning**: in-product help links include the platform version (`/docs/product/v1.9/...`).
* **Compatibility notices**: matrix pages for APIs/events with deprecation windows and migration steps.

**Release pipeline (docs CI)**

1. Validate (lint, links, a11y, spell, term checks).
2. Generate references (OpenAPI/AsyncAPI/Avro).
3. Build static sites; run Lighthouse for perf/a11y.
4. Publish to object storage + CDN (immutable by version).
5. Invalidate CDN; post summary to #docs channel.

---

# 4) CI gates & automation

**GitHub Actions (example)**

```yaml
name: docs-ci
on: [pull_request, push]
jobs:
  build:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4
      - uses: pnpm/action-setup@v3
      - run: pnpm i
      - name: Generate API refs
        run: pnpm generate:apis   # redocly + asyncapi generator
      - name: Lint & style
        run: pnpm lint:md && pnpm lint:vale && pnpm lint:links
      - name: Build
        run: pnpm build:docs      # mkdocs/docusaurus
      - name: Lighthouse
        run: pnpm test:lighthouse
      - name: Upload artifact
        uses: actions/upload-pages-artifact@v3
```

**Required checks**: broken links=0, a11y pass ≥ 98%, Vale style pass, term list compliance, API/AsyncAPI present for changed contracts.

---

# 5) Content models (front-matter)

```yaml
title: Create an ECO with effectivity
audience: engineer
persona: product-engineer
lifecycle: Deliver
est_time: 7m
permissions: [change.write, approve.sign]
min_version: 1.9.0
last_verified: 2025-11-05
tags: [change, effectivity, baseline]
```

---

# 6) Templates (copy/paste)

## 6.1 How-to (task)

```
# Goal
Explain outcome + why it matters (1–2 sentences).

# Before you start
• Role/permissions • Baseline/variant context • Risks • Time

# Steps
1) ...
2) ...
> Tip: ...
> Caution: ...

# Verify
What success looks like + where to check.

# Roll back
Exact steps to undo.

# Next
Related tasks, references, FAQs.
```

## 6.2 Troubleshooting

```
# Symptoms
Errors, log lines, screenshots.

# Probable causes
1) Cause A
2) Cause B

# Fix
Stepwise command + expected outputs.

# Prevent
Policy change or configuration.
```

## 6.3 Runbook

* Symptom → Impact → Immediate action (copy/paste) → Diagnostics (queries) → Remediation → Prevention → Owners.

## 6.4 ADR

* Context → Decision → Alternatives → Consequences → Status → Review date.

## 6.5 Connector guide

* Supported versions, auth, scopes, rate limits, field mappings, idempotency keys, golden payloads, sandbox instructions.

---

# 7) Content types (by audience)

### Product users/admins

* **Task guides** (short), **concepts** (short, diagram first), **reference** (field tables, limits), **tutorials** (guided, sample data), **release notes**.

### Developers/integrators

* **API & event refs**, **SDK tutorials**, **contract tests**, **golden datasets**, **mapping DSL** examples, **webhook replay** instructions.

### SRE/ops

* **Runbooks**, **SLO catalogs**, **topology** snapshots, **incident templates**, **game-day scripts**.

### Compliance/auditors

* **Evidence pack structure**, **hash/signature verification**, **baseline rehydrate**, **standard mappings** pages.

### Partners/Marketplace

* **Publishing guide**, **certification checklist**, **permission catalog**, **billing/metering spec**, **sample extension** walkthroughs.

---

# 8) Media & examples pipeline

* Screenshots/recordings auto-captured by Playwright + scripted data → reviewed → optimized (WebP, <300KB).
* GIF length < 12s; caption + alt text required; dark & light variants.
* Redaction: automatic blurring of IDs, emails, tenant names; watermarks for external docs.

---

# 9) Style, terminology, inclusivity

* **Vale** rules: sentence length ≤ 25 words; passive voice < 10%; forbidden jargon list (with suggested terms).
* **Word list** (canonical): ECO, ECR, baseline, twin, effectivity, evidence pack, NCR, CAPA, SPC, SBOM, etc., with one-line definitions.
* **Tone**: direct, active, imperative; verb-first buttons and headings.
* **Localization**: ICU messages; avoid idioms; units in SI with localized display.

---

# 10) Search & discoverability

* Site search boosts: exact ID matches (e.g., `ECO-1234`) > titles > headings > body.
* Synonym lists (e.g., “BOM” ~ “bill of materials”).
* No-result auto-issues: top failed queries open triage tickets weekly.

---

# 11) Governance & ownership

**RACI**

* **Product area owner**: accuracy.
* **Tech writer**: clarity, structure, style.
* **Compliance**: evidence & legal.
* **SRE**: runbooks, SLOs.
* **Security**: redaction & export control.

**Review cadence**

* Runbooks & cluster ops: **90 days**.
* High-traffic how-tos: **180 days**.
* Low-change concepts: **annual**.
* Auto-open PRs when `last_verified` exceeds SLA.

---

# 12) Compliance, export control, and audit

* Export-controlled pages flagged in front-matter `export_control: true`; external site excludes them.
* Evidence docs always **baseline-pinned** and **hash-signed**; include verifier commands.
* **WORM** storage for published evidence; retention policies shown on each page.

**Verifier example**

```bash
evidence verify --manifest pack.json \
  --baseline B42 \
  --sig dsse.sig
# Output: OK (sha256: 4c1e…)
```

---

# 13) In-product help & UI integration

* Each route declares a **help key**; shell injects `?` panel with the matching doc (role-aware).
* Command palette surfaces top tasks (“Generate Evidence Pack — guide”).
* Tooltips link to glossary entries (hovercards).
* “Was this helpful?” feedback widget → GitHub issue with context (url, role, locale, version).

---

# 14) Metrics, KPIs & analytics

* **Findability**: Search success ≥ 85% (no bounce in 30s).
* **Freshness**: 95% pages `last_verified ≤ 180d`; runbooks ≤ 90d.
* **Coverage**: every GA feature has: how-to + concept + reference + troubleshooting.
* **Quality**: Doc NPS ≥ 60; tutorial completion ≥ 80%.
* **Localization**: top 3 locales within 2 versions of English.

**Instrumentation**

* Page view + time-to-first-answer (TTFA ~ time until copy interaction or external link click).
* Search queries/success; broken link counts; feedback ratio.

---

# 15) Security & privacy in docs

* **Never** include secrets, internal hostnames, or real tenant data.
* Synthetic datasets for screenshots and tutorials.
* Redaction bot runs in CI; blocks PRs with leaked tokens/IDs via regex + entropy detection.

# 16) Example content (ready to paste)

## 16.1 How-to: Generate a V&V Evidence Pack

**Goal**
Create a signed V&V pack for baseline **B42** to share with an auditor.

**Before you start**

* Role: Approver or Compliance
* Baseline exists and trace coverage ≥ 90%
* Time: ~2 minutes

**Steps**

1. Go to **Deliver → Evidence** → **New Pack**.
2. Choose **Baseline** = *B42*, **Standard** = *ISO 26262 – ASIL B*.
3. Select **Scope** (project *Apollo*, components *Brake*, *ABS*).
4. Click **Generate**. Wait for **Signed** badge.

**Verify**
Download `pack.json` and run:

```bash
evidence verify --manifest pack.json
```

Expect: `OK (hash: …)` and signers list.

**Roll back**
Delete the pack (keeps baseline) and regenerate.

**Next**
“Submit pack for review” • “Add to compliance gate”

## 16.2 Connector mapping table (Jira → Requirement)

| Jira field                   | Platform field         | Transform             |
| ---------------------------- | ---------------------- | --------------------- |
| `issue.fields.summary`       | `requirement.title`    | passthrough           |
| `issue.fields.description`   | `requirement.text`     | sanitize_md()         |
| `issue.fields.priority.name` | `requirement.priority` | lookup(priority)      |
| `issue.fields.custom.reqid`  | `requirement.id`       | ensure_prefix("REQ-") |

3. **Evidence reproducibility**: auditor follows doc to re-verify a pack; signatures & hashes match.
4. **Search success**: querying “effectivity” yields the how-to within top 3; click-through ≥ 70% in telemetry.
5. **Runbook freshness**: all SRE runbooks show `last_verified ≤ 90d`; CI fails if not.
6. **Export control**: restricted pages are excluded from public build automatically.
